- <section class="LayoutSectionstyles__Layout-sc-1ny73ll-0 ckruOD"><div class="ContentContainerstyles__Container-sc-1jtnn3b-0 daIRbn TextBlockSEO_text-block-seo__ANhVa"><h1 data-test="markup" class="markup heading-05-bold"><i>Star Wars</i>™ Toys & Sets</h1><p class="body-sm-regular"><span><span data-test="text-truncate" class="TextTruncate_text__32VE9 undefined" style="font-size:var(--st-font-size-sm1);line-height:var(--st-line-height-sm1);max-height:calc(var(--st-line-height-sm1) * 3);-webkit-line-clamp:3"><span>One of the most popular franchises in the world, Star Wars™, has been one with the Force since 1977 - and our LEGO® Star Wars™ sets bring the &quot;galaxy far, far away&quot; a whole lot closer. With your favorite LEGO® Star Wars™ sets and figures, you can join the Jedi or the Sith and battle between the light and dark side of The Force whilst recreating scenes from the <a href="/en-us/categories/movies">movies</a> with all your favorite <a href="/en-us/themes/star-wars/characters">characters</a> such as Luke Skywalker, Yoda, Grogu, Darth Vader, Emperor Palpatine, Princess Leia, Han Solo, Chewbacca, R2-D2, C-3PO and more. Or, for more skilled builders, you can build Star Wars™ ships or create your own <a href="/en-us/themes/star-wars/helmets">Star Wars™ helmet</a>, Imperial Star Destroyer™ or AT-AT™. LEGO Star Wars™ buildable construction toys and <a href="/en-us/themes/minifigures">minifigures</a> are inspired by classic Star Wars™ comic books and action-packed movies from <a href="/en-us/themes/star-wars/games/skywalker-saga">The Skywalker Saga</a> and beyond, and <a href="/en-us/categories/lego-sets-inspired-by-tv">TV shows</a> such as <a href="/en-us/themes/star-wars/mandalorian">The Mandalorian™</a>, Droids, Star Wars: The Clone Wars, The Book of Boba Fett. Our exciting collection contains the best <a href="/en-us/gifts">gifts</a> for <a href="/en-us/toys-for-girls">girls</a> and <a href="/en-us/toys-for-boys">boys</a> <a href="/en-us/categories/age-6-plus-years">aged 6+</a>, and <a href="/en-us/categories/adults-welcome">adults</a> who love all things Star Wars™. If you&#39;re a dedicated LEGO® Star Wars™ fan, check out our <a href="/en-us/categories/ultimate-collector-series">Ultimate Collector Series</a>, filled with <a href="/en-us/categories/hard-to-find">hard-to-find</a>, truly impressive sets! Explore our other movie sets too, including the latest <a href="/en-us/themes/indiana-jones/about">Indiana Jones™</a> range!</span></span></span></p>
